            RESOLUTION BROADENING.                                2011601600011 
           .PROGRAM I  YIELDS THE FOLOWING PARAMETERS,            2011601600012

             THE TOTAL WIDTH (I),                                 2011601600014 
             THE PARAMETER((G*NEUTRON-WIDTH)*(FISSION-WIDTH)/     2011601600015 
                   (TOTAL-WIDTH I)) = FISSION AREA * LAMBDA**(-2),2011601600016 
             WHERE LAMBDA IS THE NEUTRON WAVE LENGTH.             2011601600017 
           .PROGRAM II  EXTRACTS THE FOLLOWING PARAMETERS,        2011601600018 
             THE RESONANCE ENERGY (II),                           2011601600019 
             THE TOTAL WIDTH (II),                                2011601600020 
             THE NEUTRON WIDTH TIMES 2G.                          2011601600021 
           .METHOD (B) TO RUN PROGRAM II WITH FIXED PARAMETERS    2011601600022 
            (TOTAL-WIDTH (I)).  THE RESULTING (2G*NEUTRON-WIDTH)  2011601600023
